36:7 So Вғ ВҠ ВҖ inheritance of ВҖ Ві of ВЈ remove Вҡ tribe to tribe: В„ ГӮ В® of ВҖ Ві of ВЈ Вғ keep himself to ВҖ inheritance of ВҖ tribe of ВҶ fathers. {keep...: В“. cleave to ВҖ, etc}
36:8 ВҒ ГӮ daughter, ВӮ possesseth an inheritance in Гһ tribe of ВҖ Ві of ВЈ, Вғ be wife В… В® of ВҖ family of ВҖ tribe of ВҜ ГҚ, ВӮ ВҖ Ві of ВЈ Г’ enjoy ГӮ ВЎ ВҖ inheritance of ВҶ fathers.
36:9 Neither Вғ ВҖ inheritance remove Вҡ {В®} tribe to another tribe; В• ГӮ В® of ВҖ tribes of ВҖ Ві of ВЈ Вғ keep himself to ВҶ own inheritance.
36:10 Вҝ as ВҖ ВҮ commanded Moses, so Г• ВҖ daughters of Zelophehad:
36:11 В„ Mahlah, Tirzah, ВҒ Hoglah, ВҒ Milcah, ВҒ Noah, ВҖ daughters of Zelophehad, Вҹ married В… В” ГҚ's brothers' ГҢ:
36:12 {ВҒ} ВҲ Вҹ married Вӯ ВҖ families of ВҖ ГҢ of Manasseh ВҖ ВҘ of Joseph, ВҒ В” inheritance remained in ВҖ tribe of ВҖ family of В” ГҚ. {Вӯ...: В“. to some ВӮ Вҹ of ВҖ families}
36:13 ГҶ {Вӣ} ВҖ commandments ВҒ ВҖ judgments, В’ ВҖ ВҮ commanded by ВҖ Вә of Moses В… ВҖ Ві of ВЈ in ВҖ plains of Moab by Jordan {near} Jericho.
